[30;1m58 | [0m[35m## split_file.py[0m
[30;1m59 | [0m[35mThis script splits one Fortran source file into several files, each containing[0m

[30;1m168 | [0m[35mFparser sets a default `NullHandler`. This prevents missing handler errors but[0m
[30;1m169 | [0m[35malso eats all logged messages. You will need to add additional handlers if you[0m
[30;1m170 | [0m[35mwish to do something with these messages.[0m
[30;1m171 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m172 | [0m[35mIf you want to intercept fparser's messages and handle them as part of your own[0m
[30;1m173 | [0m[35mlogging regime you will need to write a handler which repeats them::[0m

[30;1m58 | [0m[35m    # than "return", it will be called a second time after the test has[0m
[30;1m59 | [0m[35m    # completed. Thus anything appearing after the "yield" is teardown which[0m
[30;1m60 | [0m[35m    # happens after the test.[0m
[30;1m61 | [0m[35m    logger.removeHandler(handler)[0m
